INDEX I TO HEARINGS OF THE SPECIAL SENATE COM- 
MITTEE TO INVESTIGATE ORGANIZED CRIME IN 
INTERSTATE COMMERCE 

Index I includes the following volumes of hearings held by the 
Special Committee To Investigate Organized Crime in Interstate 
Commerce, prior to ]Mav 1, 1951. 

Part 1. Florida. 

Part lA. Florida. 

Part 2. Federal and State Officials; California Crime Commis- 
sion; Chicago Crime Commission 

Part 3. Black-Market Operations. 

Part 4. Missouri. 

Part 4A. Missouri. 

Part 5. Illinois. 

Part 6. Ohio — Kentucky. 

Part 7. New York — New Jersey. 

Part 8. Louisiana. 

Part 9. Michigan. 

Part 10. Nevada — California. 

Part 11. Pennsylvania. 

Part 12. Federal and State Officials, and Miscellaneous Wit- 
' nesses. 
The fact that a name appears in this index is not necessarily au 
indication of a record of criminal activities. It simply indicates that 
said name has been mentioned in connection with testimony or printed 
exhibits. A careful check of the references in the text of the hearing 
will determine the circumstances under which such person is named.
